Billboard_logo.svg Wonder_Girls_in_San_Francisco_Jun_13_2010.jpg, The Fillmore, San Francisco, June 13, 2010]] LIST OF K-POP SONGS ON THE _BILLBOARD_ CHARTS is a compilation of chart information for K-pop music published by the _Billboard_ charts, and reported on by _Billboard K-Town_, an online _Billboard_ column. This is a list of K-pop SONGS and singles on the _Billboard_ charts.[1][2]


2001 – present

-   This list depends on continual updates taken from *[3] and *.[4]
-   Charts with all updates 2009–present are marked (Complete).
-   _Billboard_ artists comprehensive update incomplete.
-   _Billboard_ charts comprehensive update incomplete.
-   The list is currently minus portions of Psy performance on 58 charts.
-   The list is exclusive of Korea K-Pop Hot 100 data.
-   Figures in red highlight indicate the highest rating received by K-pop artists on that chart.
-   – Current week's charting
